12/04/24, 2:51 pm - +91 80929 56210: #include <stdio.h>

void selection_sort(int *arr, int n) {
    int i, j, min_index, temp;
    
    for (i = 0; i < n - 1; i++) {
        min_index = i;
        for (j = i + 1; j < n; j++) {
            if (arr[j] < arr[min_index]) {
                min_index = j;
            }
        }
        if (min_index != i) {
            // Swap arr[i] and arr[min_index]
            temp = arr[i];
            arr[i] = arr[min_index];
            arr[min_index] = temp;
        }
    }
}

int main() {
    int n, i;

    printf("Enter the number of elements in the array: ");
    scanf("%d", &n);

    int arr[n];

    printf("Enter %d elements:\n", n);
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        scanf("%d", &arr[i]);
    }

    printf("Original array: ");
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        printf("%d ", arr[i]);
    }
    printf("\n");

    selection_sort(arr, n);

    printf("Sorted array: ");
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        printf("%d ", arr[i]);
    }
    printf("\n");

    return 0;
}
12/04/24, 2:51 pm - +91 80929 56210: #include <stdio.h>

void modified_bubble_sort(char *arr, int n) {
    int i, j;
    char temp;
    int swapped;

    for (i = 0; i < n-1; i++) {
        swapped = 0;
        for (j = 0; j < n-i-1; j++) {
            if (arr[j] > arr[j+1]) {
                // Swap elements
                temp = arr[j];
                arr[j] = arr[j+1];
                arr[j+1] = temp;
                swapped = 1;
            }
        }
        // If no two elements were swapped, array is sorted
        if (swapped == 0) 
            break;
    }
}

int main() {
    int n;
    printf("Enter the number of elements in the array: ");
    scanf("%d", &n);
    
    char arr[n];
    printf("Enter the elements of the array:\n");
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        scanf(" %c", &arr[i]);
    }
    
    modified_bubble_sort(arr, n);
    
    printf("Sorted array: ");
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        printf("%c ", arr[i]);
    }
    printf("\n");
    
    return 0;
}
12/04/24, 2:51 pm - +91 80929 56210: #include <stdio.h>

void insertion_sort(char *arr, int n) {
    int i, j;
    char key;

    for (i = 1; i < n; i++) {
        key = arr[i];
        j = i - 1;

        // Move elements of arr[0..i-1], that are greater than key,
        // to one position ahead of their current position
        while (j >= 0 && arr[j] > key) {
            arr[j + 1] = arr[j];
            j = j - 1;
        }
        arr[j + 1] = key;
    }
}

int main() {
    int n;
    printf("Enter the number of elements in the array: ");
    scanf("%d", &n);
    
    char arr[n];
    printf("Enter the elements of the array:\n");
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        scanf(" %c", &arr[i]);
    }
    
    insertion_sort(arr, n);
    
    printf("Sorted array: ");
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        printf("%c ", arr[i]);
    }
    printf("\n");
    
    return 0;
}

22/07/24, 11:54 am - Bharadwaj IITP: Dear Students,

The process of course registration in Autumn 2024 semester is as follows:

Steps of Registration, Autumn Semester 2024
Date: 22.07.2024
Time: 12.00 PM onwards
VENUE: Office of Department Faculty Advisor
Step 1: Student will submit copy of fee payment receipt (please write Name and Roll no., and Program on it). Students, applicable for B. Tech. only) claiming tuition fee exemption/relaxation on the basis of annual income must submit the undertaking signed by their parents/guardian along with their income certificate issued on or after April 01, 2024. 
Step 2: Students (Only B. Tech., M. Tech., and M. Sc.) will register for their respective courses on Moodle using the following link:
https://ais.iitp.ac.in/moodle/
Students need to change their current semester number (Sem III/V/VII as applicable) by editing their profile under the program details on Moodle prior registering for the courses. 
Steps for changing current semester: Click on Profile (Top right corner)-> Edit Profile-> Scroll down and Open Program Details-> Change your current semester. 
The course registration process for Ph. D. students will be shared soon via separate email by 24th July once the appropriate courses will be populated on the portal (http://172.16.1.230/).
Step 3: Student will submit course registration slip and fee payment receipt to Faculty Advisor. The faculty advisor will verify and put his/her signature on the course registration slip. The faculty advisors for B. Tech. 2022 Batch are requested to ensure that the students have cleared all the first-year courses before registering for semester V courses. 
Step 4: On completion of above steps only, Faculty Advisor would confirm registration completion after fee verification. The students will put their signature on a sheet available with Faculty Advisor.
@Faculty Advisor: Please ensure that all the documents are submitted to the academic section after completion of registration process.

Thanks

PIC Registration
22/07/24, 12:08 pm - Bharadwaj IITP: Dear Students,
 
We are glad to inform you that from this year, the Departments are going to offer Minor Program (a total of about 18 programs. In general, a total credit of 16 / 17 is allocated for Minor Program). The courses are floated from Semester III to VII in the revised course curriculum). The students would be allowed to register in Minor Courses based on their merits. 
 
@heads_academic
 
Based on 28th Senate decision, the following points is to be taken care of :
 
Department may intake 20% of their approved strength (B. Tech. program) for minor degree.
Department should also clearly mention compatible branches and pre-requisites for their minor courses. (in the form the Department would generate)
Students with CPI> 7.5 may be offered minor courses (again, this depends on seat availability and merit).
If student (taking minor courses) fails to maintain CPI or SPI > 7.5 (from 5th Semester onwards), then their minor will be automatically cancelled.
If student could not finish their minor courses at their time of completing of bachelor's degree (from their parent Department), they won't be getting any kind of certificate / degree for Minor.
 
It is therefore, requested to kindly circulate a form mentioning the options for Minor Courses in their respective Department. Further, the eligible students (based on merit and compatible branches set by the Department ) would submit a signed hard copy to the Department. The Department would thus generate a merit list complying the above stated points within a week (02nd August, 2024). Finally, the students would be allowed to register for their choice of Minor on moodle. 
 
The details of revised fees for Minor would be intimated in due course of time (if required).
 
Regards, 
 
 
विजय कुमार 

Vijay Kumar 

उप कुलसचिव (शैक्षणिक) 
Deputy Registrar (Academics) 

आईआईटी पटना 
IIT Patna 
06115233784

13/11/24, 9:22 am - Prashant Room: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <algorithm>

using namespace std;

struct Edge {
    int u, v, weight;
};

bool compareEdges(Edge a, Edge b) {
    return a.weight < b.weight;
}

int findParent(int u, vector<int> &parent) {
    if (u != parent[u])
        parent[u] = findParent(parent[u], parent);
    return parent[u];
}

void unionSets(int u, int v, vector<int> &parent, vector<int> &rank) {
    u = findParent(u, parent);
    v = findParent(v, parent);
    if (rank[u] < rank[v]) {
        parent[u] = v;
    } else if (rank[u] > rank[v]) {
        parent[v] = u;
    } else {
        parent[v] = u;
        rank[u]++;
    }
}

void constructMST(int n, vector<Edge> &edges) {
    sort(edges.begin(), edges.end(), compareEdges);
    vector<int> parent(n), rank(n, 0);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) parent[i] = i;

    int mstWeight = 0;
    vector<Edge> mstEdges;

    for (Edge edge : edges) {
        if (findParent(edge.u, parent) != findParent(edge.v, parent)) {
            mstWeight += edge.weight;
            mstEdges.push_back(edge);
            unionSets(edge.u, edge.v, parent, rank);
            if (mstEdges.size() == n - 1) break;
        }
    }

    cout << "Minimum Spanning Tree constructed with weight: " << mstWeight << endl;
    cout << "Edges in the MST:" << endl;
    for (Edge edge : mstEdges) {
        cout << edge.u << " - " << edge.v << " (Weight: " << edge.weight << ")" << endl;
    }
}

int main() {
    int n = 5; // Number of vertices

    // Define edges of the graph G
    vector<Edge> edges = {
        {0, 1, 1}, {0, 4, 2}, {1, 2, 5}, {2, 3, 4}, {3, 4, 3},
        {0, 2, 6}, {0, 3, 7}, {1, 4, 8}, {2, 4, 10}, {1, 3, 9}
    };

    constructMST(n, edges);

    return 0;
}
